				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					15 Inventions, BWV 772-786 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div><table style="padding:0.5em; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto; background-color:rgb(245,245,245); width:70%; border:1px solid #a3bfb1"><tr><td width="42px" valign="top"><a href="/wiki/File:Ambox_notice.png" class="image"><img alt="Ambox notice.png" src="/images/c/c8/Ambox_notice.png" width="40" height="40" /></a></td><td align="center">
This page is <b>only</b> for <b>complete</b> editions and <b>multiple selections</b> from the collection here. For arrangements, new editions, and the like see (or create) separate pages for individual works linked in the <b>General Information</b> section below.</td></tr></table></div>
<div><table style="padding:0.25em; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto; background-color:rgb(245,245,245); width:80%; border:1px solid #a3bfb1"><tr><td width="42px" valign="top"><a href="/wiki/File:Ambox_notice.png" class="image"><img alt="Ambox notice.png" src="/images/c/c8/Ambox_notice.png" width="40" height="40" /></a></td><td align="left"><center>For the later set of 15 Sinfonias (3-part inventions), see <i><a href="/wiki/15_Sinfonias,_BWV_787-801_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="15 Sinfonias, BWV 787-801 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">15 Sinfonias, BWV 787-801</a></i>.</center></td></tr></table></div>
<p><br />
</p>
<div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>15 inventions
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1720–23 in <i><a href="/wiki/Inventions_and_Sinfonias,_BWV_772-801_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Inventions and Sinfonias, BWV 772-801 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Inventions and Sinfonias</a></i>
</td></tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">15 Inventions
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 772-786&#160;; BC L27–41
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 330
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>15 inventions:
<ol><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Invention_in_C_major,_BWV_772_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Invention in C major, BWV 772 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Invention in C major, BWV 772</a></i>
</li><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Invention_in_C_minor,_BWV_773_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Invention in C minor, BWV 773 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Invention in C minor, BWV 773</a></i>
</li><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Invention_in_D_major,_BWV_774_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Invention in D major, BWV 774 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Invention in D major, BWV 774</a></i>
</li><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Invention_in_D_minor,_BWV_775_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Invention in D minor, BWV 775 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Invention in D minor, BWV 775</a></i>
</li><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Invention_in_E-flat_major,_BWV_776_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Invention in E-flat major, BWV 776 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Invention in E-flat major, BWV 776</a></i>
